Ayuda a desarrollar el pensamiento y mejora la memoria y la atención. La aplicación tiene tres modos de juego: por números, letras y colores. Los modos de juego con letras y números serán útiles para los niños de jardín de niños y maternal. \r\n La conexión de números les ayudará a que memoricen fácilmente el orden de los números y que aprendan a contar. Para ello, deben conectar consecutivamente círculos con números a partir de 1. Cuando conecten círculos en el orden correcto, la silueta de una imagen oculta se volverá cada vez más visible. Si eligen tres puntos incorrectamente, aparecerá una sugerencia. Una vez que todos los puntos estén completamente conectados, la imagen se volverá totalmente visible y podrán colorearla. \r\n Aquellos niños que estudian el alfabeto pueden elegir conectar puntos por medio de letras. Es importante que los niños conozcan las letras lo antes posible, ya que es esencial para que aprendan a leer y escribir. ¡Pero conocer el orden de las letras en el alfabeto es también muy importante! It has been used for generations, and proven its success over and over again. Our second memory device, the memory palace, is one of the oldest and most successful tools in the book! This method goes back to the ancient Greeks, and involves imagining a familiar environment (like your home) and associating the things to be remembered with particular areas or aspects of that environment.  The visual and spatial qualities of this form provide additional contact points that aid in the creation of cognitive associations with the thing that we want to remember. This creates more access routes for our brains to get at the desired information, and thus increases ease of recall. The bid number is the number of tricks (books) a player believes his partnership can achieve over 6. For example, a bid of 4 = 10 books. \r\n\r\nThe bid description indicates a bid direction (High or Low) or whether the bid is a 'No' trump. A bid direction of High (Uptown) indicates A,K,Q... are the highest value cards. A bid direction of Low (Downtown, Special) indicates A,2,3... are the highest value cards. A 'No' trump bid indicates that each suit has equal weight and the lead card can not be 'cut'.  The bid direction of a 'No' bid is specified after winning the bid.\r\nBid numbers can range from 3 - 7.  The Option screen gives the player the option of playing with a minimum of 3 or 4.\r\nBid descriptions have the following weights:  'No' > 'Low' > 'High'.  The Option screen allows the player to play make 'Low' and 'High' equal in weight: 'No' > 'Low' = 'High'. \r\n\r\nThe highest bidder indicates a 'trump' suit or in the case of a 'No' bid indicates the direction (High/Low).  The jokers become the highest value cards in the indicated 'trump' suit. In the case of a 'No' bid, the Big Joker and Little Joker have no value and should be discarded as soon as possible.\r\n\r\nThe bid winner will start play as the lead player.
